\"DrainManagerImpl::startDrainSequence\"}\n  ],\n  \"text\": \"The Envoy listener manager is implemented across multiple C++ source files in the envoyproxy/envoy repository, organized into several functional layers:\\n\\n## Core Listener Manager\\nThe primary listener manager implementation resides in `source/common/listener_manager/listener_manager_impl.h/cc`. The `ListenerManagerImpl` class implements the `ListenerManager` interface and manages the complete listener lifecycle including:\\n- Listener addition and removal via `addOrUpdateListener()` and `removeListener()` methods\\n- Listener draining through the `drainListener()` method, which uses the `DrainingFilterChainsManager` class\\n- Listener initialization and state management for warming, active, and draining listeners\\n- Worker thread assignment via `addListenerToWorker()` method\\n- Worker startup coordination through `startWorkers()` method\\n\\n## Listener Configuration\\nThe `ListenerImpl` class in `source/common/listener_manager/listener_impl.h/cc` maps protobuf listener configuration to runtime configuration. It handles:\\n- Socket factory management through `ListenSocketFactoryImpl`, which creates and shares sockets across worker threads\\n- Socket distribution to workers via `getListenSocket()` method that returns worker-specific socket instances\\n- Support for both `reuse_port` and socket duplication modes\\n- Filter chain management through its integration with `FilterChainManagerImpl`\\n\\n## Active Listener Components\\nMultiple active listener implementations handle different protocol types and manage connection acceptance:\\n\\n1. **TCP Listeners** (`source/common/listener_manager/active_tcp_listener.h/cc`): \\n   - `ActiveTcpListener` class manages TCP connections and implements `Network::TcpListenerCallbacks`\\n   - Handles connection balancing through `post()` method for cross-worker distribution\\n   - Tracks per-listener connection counts\\n\\n2. **Stream Listener Base** (`source/common/listener_manager/active_stream_listener_base.h/cc`):\\n   - `ActiveStreamListenerBase` provides common functionality for stream-oriented listeners\\n   - `OwnedActiveStreamListenerBase` manages active connections grouped by filter chain\\n   - Handles listener filter processing and connection draining\\n\\n3. **TCP Sockets** (`source/common/listener_manager/active_tcp_socket.h/cc`):\\n   - `ActiveTcpSocket` manages accepted sockets during listener filter processing\\n   - Implements `Network::ListenerFilterManager` and `Network::ListenerFilterCallbacks`\\n\\n4. **UDP Listeners** (`source/server/active_udp_listener.h/cc` and `source/common/listener_manager/active_raw_udp_listener_config.h/cc`):\\n   - `ActiveUdpListener` handles UDP connections\\n   - `ActiveRawUdpListenerFactory` creates UDP listener instances\\n\\n5. **QUIC Listeners** (`source/common/quic/active_quic_listener.h/cc`):\\n   - `ActiveQuicListener` handles QUIC protocol connections\\n\\n6. **Internal Listeners** (`source/extensions/bootstrap/internal_listener/active_internal_listener.h/cc`):\\n   - `ActiveInternalListener` manages internal communication channels\\n\\n## Worker Thread Management\\nThe connection handler and worker implementations manage thread assignment:\\n\\n1. **Connection Handler** (`source/common/listener_manager/connection_handler_impl.h/cc`):\\n   - `ConnectionHandlerImpl` manages active listeners per worker thread\\n   - Maintains listener maps by tag and address for efficient lookup\\n   - Implements `addListener()`, `removeListeners()`, and `removeFilterChains()` methods\\n   - Tracks per-handler connection counts and listener state\\n\\n2. **Workers** (`source/server/worker_impl.h/cc`):\\n   - `WorkerImpl` represents a worker thread with its own event dispatcher\\n   - `ProdWorkerFactory` creates worker instances\\n   - functional layers:\\n\\n## Core Listener Manager\\nThe primary listener manager implementation resides in `source/common/listener_manager/listener_manager_impl.h/cc`. The `ListenerManagerImpl` class implements the `ListenerManager` interface and manages the complete listener lifecycle including:\\n- Listener addition and removal via `addOrUpdateListener()` and `removeListener()` methods\\n- Listener draining through the `drainListener()` method, which uses the `DrainingFilterChainsManager` class\\n- Listener initialization and state management for warming, active, and draining listeners\\n- Worker thread assignment via `addListenerToWorker()` method\\n- Worker startup coordination through `startWorkers()` method\\n\\n## Listener Configuration\\nThe `ListenerImpl` class in `source/common/listener_manager/listener_impl.h/cc` maps protobuf listener configuration to runtime configuration. It handles:\\n- Socket factory management through `ListenSocketFactoryImpl`, which creates and shares sockets across worker threads\\n- Socket distribution to workers via `getListenSocket()` method that returns worker-specific socket instances\\n- Support for both `reuse_port` and socket duplication modes\\n- Filter chain management through its integration with `FilterChainManagerImpl`\\n\\n## Active Listener Components\\nMultiple active listener implementations handle different protocol types and manage connection acceptance:\\n\\n1. **TCP Listeners** (`source/common/listener_manager/active_tcp_listener.h/cc`): \\n   - `ActiveTcpListener` class manages TCP connections and implements `Network::TcpListenerCallbacks`\\n   - Handles connection balancing through `post()` method for cross-worker distribution\\n   - Tracks per-listener connection counts\\n\\n2. **Stream Listener Base** (`source/common/listener_manager/active_stream_listener_base.h/cc`):\\n   - `ActiveStreamListenerBase` provides common functionality for stream-oriented listeners\\n   - `OwnedActiveStreamListenerBase` manages active connections grouped by filter chain\\n   - Handles listener filter processing and connection draining\\n\\n3. **TCP Sockets** (`source/common/listener_manager/active_tcp_socket.h/cc`):\\n   - `ActiveTcpSocket` manages accepted sockets during listener filter processing\\n   - Implements `Network::ListenerFilterManager` and `Network::ListenerFilterCallbacks`\\n\\n4. **UDP Listeners** (`source/server/active_udp_listener.h/cc` and `source/common/listener_manager/active_raw_udp_listener_config.h/cc`):\\n   - `ActiveUdpListener` handles UDP connections\\n   - `ActiveRawUdpListenerFactory` creates UDP listener instances\\n\\n5. **QUIC Listeners** (`source/common/quic/active_quic_listener.h/cc`):\\n   - `ActiveQuicListener` handles QUIC protocol connections\\n\\n6. **Internal Listeners** (`source/extensions/bootstrap/internal_listener/active_internal_listener.h/cc`):\\n   - `ActiveInternalListener` manages internal communication channels\\n\\n## Worker Thread Management\\nThe connection handler and worker implementations manage thread assignment:\\n\\n1. **Connection Handler** (`source/common/listener_manager/connection_handler_impl.h/cc`):\\n   - `ConnectionHandlerImpl` manages active listeners per worker thread\\n   - Maintains listener maps by tag and address for efficient lookup\\n   - Implements `addListener()`, `removeListeners()`, and `removeFilterChains()` methods\\n   - Tracks per-handler connection counts and listener state\\n\\n2. **Workers** (`source/server/worker_impl.h/cc`):\\n   - `WorkerImpl` represents a worker thread with its own event dispatcher\\n   - `ProdWorkerFactory` creates worker instances\\n   - Workers receive listener add/remove requests through `addListener()` and `removeListener()` methods\\n   - Filter chains can be removed dynamically via `removeFilterChains()`\\n\\n## Socket Sharing Between Workers\\nSocket sharing is implemented through:\\n- `ListenSocketFactoryImpl` in `listener_impl.h/cc` which maintains a vector of sockets, one per worker\\n- Support for two modes: socket duplication (no `reuse_port`) or unique sockets per worker (`reuse_port`)\\n- The `getListenSocket(worker_index)` method returns the appropriate socket for each worker\\n- `ProdListenerComponentFactory::createListenSocket()` handles socket creation with worker index awareness\\n\\n## Listener Draining Mechanism\\nThe drain mechanism is implemented through:\\n\\n1. **Drain Manager** (`source/server/drain_manager_impl.h/cc`):\\n   - `DrainManagerImpl` manages the drain sequence for listeners\\n   - `startDrainSequence()` initiates draining with configurable timeouts\\n   - Supports drain type configuration (GRACEFUL, IMMEDIATE)\\n\\n2. **Filter Chain Draining** (`source/common/listener_manager/listener_manager_impl.h/cc`):\\n   - `DrainingFilterChainsManager` tracks filter chains being drained\\n   - `drainFilterChains()` method initiates draining of specific filter chains\\n   - Supports in-place filter chain updates where only changed chains are drained\\n\\n## Dynamic Listener Configuration\\nThe LDS API implementation in `source/common/listener_manager/lds_api.h/cc` provides:\\n- `LdsApiImpl` class for dynamic listener discovery\\n- Subscription-based updates to listeners\\n- Integration with cluster manager for resource fetching\\n\\n## Filter Chain Management\\nThe `FilterChainManagerImpl` in `source/common/listener_manager/filter_chain_manager_impl.h/cc` handles:\\n- Filter chain selection based on connection properties\\n- Efficient matching using destination ports, IPs, server names, and protocols\\n- Filter chain draining during listener updates\\n\\n## Factory and Extension Points\\nThe listener manager architecture is extensible through:\\n- `ListenerManagerFactory` (source/server/listener_manager_factory.h) for pluggable implementations\\n- `ValidationListenerManagerFactoryImpl` (source/extensions/listener_managers/validation_listener_manager/) for configuration validation\\n- `ListenerComponentFactory` for customizable socket creation and filter factory management\\n\\nThis architecture enables Envoy to efficiently manage multiple listeners across worker threads with graceful draining, dynamic configuration updates, and protocol-specific optimizations.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
